DISTRIBUTION_NNP ._.
The_DT distribution_NN of_IN anthrax_NN in_IN this_DT Province_NNP is_VBZ widespread_JJ ._.
In_IN the_DT last_JJ two_CD years_NNS ,_, during_IN which_WDT time_NN an_DT effort_NN has_VBZ been_VBN made_VBN to_TO increase_VB the_DT number_NN of_IN blood_NN smears_NNS submitted_VBD for_IN microscopic_NN examination_NN from_IN dead_JJ animals_NNS in_IN the_DT districts_NNS ,_, the_DT disease_NN has_VBZ been_VBN recorded_VBN from_IN practically_RB every_DT district_NN ._.

As_IN examples_NNS of_IN this_DT ,_, we_PRP have_VBP the_DT recent_JJ mortality_NN (_( 1928-29_JJ )_) in_IN the_DT horses_NNS of_IN the_DT Rangoon_NNP Paper_NNP Chase_NNP Club_NNP and_CC the_DT annual_JJ epidemics_NNS which_WDT have_VBP occurred_VBN up_RP to_TO the_DT present_JJ in_IN the_DT elephants_NNS of_IN the_DT timber_NN firms_NNS ,_, working_VBG in_IN infected_JJ forest_JJS areas_NNS ._.

H_NNP CLINICAL_NNP NOTES_NNP ._.
An_DT Interesting_JJ Case_NN of_IN Cystic_NNP Calculi_NNP ._.
(_( With_IN Plate_NNP VI_NNP ._. )_)
